Before the C-terminal region of low similarity, the relative reading frames of fog-2 and ftr-1 are conserved with all insertions and deletions in three nucleotide multiples and an overall amino acid identity of 70%. Within the final exon, multiple amino acid substitutions, insertions, and deletions have occurred, resulting in a region of low nucleotide and amino acid identity (Figure 4B and 4C). For example, an indel (deletion relative to fog-2) at nucleotide 805 shifts the reading frame of FOG-2 relative to FTR-1 and results in a region of low similarity between the proteins (Figure 4B). A second indel at position 819 restores the reading frame but additional substitutions result in a diverged amino acid sequence (Figure 4C).
###end p 31
###begin p 32
###xml 428 436 428 436 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g004">Figure 4</xref>
###xml 566 574 566 574 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g004">Figure 4</xref>
###xml 618 620 618 620 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b25">25</xref>
###xml 790 798 790 798 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g004">Figure 4</xref>
###xml 1042 1063 1042 1063 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 541 546 <span type="species:ncbi:4932">yeast</span>
The dramatic differences between the FOG-2 and FTR-1 C-terminal regions suggested a connection between the unique functionality of FOG-2 in sex determination and the highly diverged C-terminal region. Since FOG-2 interacts with GLD-1 and both are required for the promotion of the male germ cell fate in the hermaphrodite, we determined whether the diverged FOG-2 C-terminal region was necessary for its interaction with GLD-1 (Figure 4). Progressive C-terminal deletions of FOG-2 were tested for their ability to interact with GLD-1 in the yeast two-hybrid system (Figure 4D). Full-length FOG-2 interacts with GLD-1 [25]; however, C-terminal deletions of nine and 28 aa in FOG-2 reduced the interaction, and deletion of 64 and 76 aa (essentially all of exon 4) eliminated the interaction (Figure 4D), indicating that the highly divergent C-terminal region is necessary for GLD-1 binding. All full-length and deletion constructs were tested against the Skp1 homolog SKR-1 as a positive control for functionality in the two-hybrid system (see Materials and Methods).
###end p 32
###begin p 33
###xml 248 250 248 250 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b25">25</xref>
###xml 253 261 253 261 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g004">Figure 4</xref>
###xml 296 301 296 301 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">ftr-1</italic>
###xml 319 324 319 324 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 369 377 369 377 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g004">Figure 4</xref>
To determine whether the C-terminal region of FOG-2 is sufficient to confer GLD-1 interaction, an FTR-1/FOG-2 exon 4 chimera was generated and assayed for its ability to interact with GLD-1. Normally FTR-1 lacks the ability to interact with GLD-1 [25] (Figure 4D). The replacement of exon 4 from ftr-1 with exon 4 from fog-2 allowed the chimera to interact with GLD-1 (Figure 4D). Thus, the C-terminal 74aa region of FOG-2, when in the context of the FTR-1 F-box and Duf38/FTH sequences, is sufficient to confer GLD-1 binding.
###end p 33
###begin title 34
###xml 43 53 43 53 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 43 53 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
FOG-2/GLD-1 Interaction Evolved Rapidly in C. elegans
###end title 34
###begin p 35
###xml 240 242 240 242 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b48">48</xref>
###xml 440 441 440 441 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</sub>
###xml 495 496 495 496 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</sub>
###xml 499 501 499 501 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b49">49</xref>
###xml 502 504 502 504 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b50">50</xref>
###xml 508 509 508 509 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</sub>
###xml 511 512 511 512 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</sub>
###xml 720 721 720 721 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</sub>
###xml 723 724 723 724 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</sub>
###xml 942 944 942 944 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b51">51</xref>
Gene duplication provides the raw material for the evolution of novel adaptations, having been implicated in the diversity of the host-pathogen immune response, rapid onset of insecticide resistance, and diversity of vertebrate body plans [48]. Rapidly evolving genes, or portions of genes, under positive selection can be identified by comparison of nucleotide alterations that result in amino acid changes (non-synonymous substitutions [Ka]) to alterations that do not change the amino acid (Ks) [49,50]. Ka/Ks ratios that are equal to or less than one are indicative of neutral or purifying selection, where substitutions that change amino acids offer no fitness advantage or result in lowered fitness. In contrast, Ka/Ks ratios greater than one, common in rapidly evolving genes, are indicative of positive selection, where non-synonymous changes offer some fitness advantage and are fixed at a higher rate than synonymous substitutions [51].
###end p 35
###begin p 36
###xml 41 52 41 52 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2/ftr-1</italic>
###xml 78 79 78 79 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</sub>
###xml 81 82 81 82 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</sub>
###xml 98 111 98 111 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2, ftr-1,</italic>
###xml 146 151 146 151 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 155 165 155 165 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 255 260 255 260 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 314 319 314 319 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 357 358 357 358 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</sub>
###xml 360 361 360 361 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</sub>
###xml 426 427 426 427 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</sub>
###xml 429 430 429 430 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</sub>
###xml 441 452 441 452 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2/ftr-1</italic>
###xml 524 525 524 525 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</sub>
###xml 527 528 527 528 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</sub>
###xml 546 548 546 548 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b52">52</xref>
###xml 554 559 554 559 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 564 569 564 569 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">ftr-1</italic>
###xml 682 683 682 683 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</sub>
###xml 685 686 685 686 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</sub>
###xml 735 743 735 743 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g004">Figure 4</xref>
###xml 806 807 806 807 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</sub>
###xml 809 810 809 810 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</sub>
###xml 829 831 829 831 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b53">53</xref>
###xml 928 949 928 949 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 155 165 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
To determine the selection acting on the fog-2/ftr-1 duplication we compared Ka/Ks ratios between fog-2, ftr-1, and the five FTR genes closest to fog-2 in C. elegans. Pairwise comparisons of codon-delimited full-length coding sequences closely related to fog-2 suggest that purifying selection dominates along the fog-2 branch, as all comparisons produced Ka/Ks ratios less than one (mean = 0.46). However, while the overall Ka/Ks ratio for fog-2/ftr-1 is not indicative of positive selection (mean = 0.58), sliding-window Ka/Ks ratio estimates [52] for fog-2 and ftr-1 indicate that the highly diverged C-terminal region of FOG-2/FTR-1 contains residues under positive selection (Ka/Ks = 1.98 for nucleotides 777-987, windows 33-37) (Figure 4). An alternate method using maximum likelihood estimation of Ka/Ks (PAML and codeml [53]) confirmed the presence of residues under positive selection within the C-terminal region (see Materials and Methods). Thus, the primary differences between FOG-2 and FTR-1 are localized to the rapidly evolving C-terminus of FOG-2 that is required for GLD-1 binding and is under positive selection.
###end p 36
###begin p 37
###xml 57 62 57 62 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 64 66 64 66 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b25">25</xref>
###xml 105 115 105 115 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 239 250 239 250 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans,</italic>
###xml 294 302 294 302 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g002">Figure 2</xref>
###xml 337 346 337 346 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g003">Figures 3</xref>
###xml 351 352 351 352 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g004">4</xref>
###xml 405 410 405 410 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 417 428 417 428 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 464 475 464 475 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 503 514 503 514 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 4 9 <span type="species:ncbi:4932">yeast</span>
###xml 105 115 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 239 249 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 417 428 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 464 475 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 503 514 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
The yeast two-hybrid data, together with the genetics of fog-2 [25], indicate that FOG-2 is unique among C. elegans FTR genes in functioning with GLD-1 in germline sex determination. Given the specificity of the FOG-2/GLD-1 interaction in C. elegans, phylogenetic analysis of FTR proteins (see Figure 2), and additional experiments (see Figures 3 and 4) that indicate that there are no close relatives of fog-2 among C. briggsae FTR genes, it is unlikely that any C. briggsae FTR protein functions with C. briggsae GLD-1 in sex determination.
###end p 37
###begin p 38
###xml 72 83 72 83 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 85 92 85 92 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pbio-0030006-t001">Table 1</xref>
###xml 165 175 165 175 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 177 185 177 185 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g005">Figure 5</xref>
###xml 226 236 226 236 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 247 258 247 258 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 434 444 434 444 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 508 519 508 519 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 535 546 535 546 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 72 83 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 165 175 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 226 236 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 247 258 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 434 444 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 508 519 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 535 546 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
In contrast with FOG-2, a highly conserved GLD-1 ortholog is present in C. briggsae (Table 1) and has a germline expression pattern essentially identical to that of C. elegans (Figure 5A, top right and middle right). In fact, C. elegans GLD-1 and C. briggsae GLD-1 share 81% amino acid identity overall and more than 90% in the maxi-KH RNA-binding region. Since FOG-2 and GLD-1 function together to promote the male germ cell fate in C. elegans hermaphrodites, this raised the question of what role, if any, C. briggsae GLD-1 plays in C. briggsae germline sex determination.
###end p 38
###begin title 39
###xml 32 42 32 42 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 47 58 47 58 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 32 42 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 47 58 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
GLD-1 Has Distinct Functions in C. elegans and C. briggsae Germline Sex Determination
###end title 39
###begin p 40
###xml 11 22 11 22 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 78 80 78 80 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b54">54</xref>
###xml 111 128 111 128 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae gld-1</italic>
###xml 138 149 138 149 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 227 248 227 248 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 276 292 276 292 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans gld-1</italic>
###xml 294 296 294 296 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b28">28</xref>
###xml 297 299 297 299 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b29">29</xref>
###xml 356 366 356 366 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 622 624 622 624 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b28">28</xref>
###xml 645 655 645 655 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 926 928 926 928 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b30">30</xref>
###xml 929 931 929 931 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b31">31</xref>
###xml 932 934 932 934 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b55">55</xref>
###xml 945 955 945 955 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 1158 1160 1158 1160 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b28">28</xref>
###xml 1161 1163 1161 1163 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b29">29</xref>
###xml 1166 1182 1166 1182 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans gld-1</italic>
###xml 1297 1307 1297 1307 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 1334 1336 1334 1336 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b28">28</xref>
###xml 1337 1339 1337 1339 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b29">29</xref>
###xml 11 22 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 111 122 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 138 149 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 276 286 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 356 366 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 645 655 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 945 955 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 1166 1176 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 1297 1307 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
To examine C. briggsae GLD-1 function in sex determination we performed RNAi [54] by injecting double-stranded C. briggsae gld-1 RNA into C. briggsae adult hermaphrodites followed by phenotypic analysis of F1 self progeny (see Materials and Methods). From genetic analysis of C. elegans gld-1 [28,29] there are two functions relevant to this study. First, C. elegans GLD-1 has an essential function in meiotic prophase progression during oogenesis. In null mutant hermaphrodites oogenic germ cells progress to pachytene and then return to the mitotic cell cycle, giving rise to ectopic proliferation and a germline tumor [28]. For this function C. elegans GLD-1 acts to spatially restrict the translation of multiple target mRNAs during oogenesis. GLD-1 oogenic target mRNAs are repressed during early meiotic prophase, but then are translated during late meiotic prophase following the loss of GLD-1 at the end of pachytene [30,31,55]. Second, C. elegans GLD-1 is necessary for the specification of the male sexual fate in the hermaphrodite germline. This function is most simply revealed as a haplo-insufficient feminization of the hermaphrodite germline [28,29]. C. elegans gld-1 has no known essential functions in male meiotic prophase progression or in XO male germline sex determination as C. elegans null males are wild-type [28,29].
###end p 40
###begin p 41
###xml 0 11 0 11 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 69 86 69 86 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae tra-2</italic>
###xml 189 199 189 199 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 221 237 221 237 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans tra-2</italic>
###xml 253 255 253 255 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b25">25</xref>
###xml 305 315 305 315 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 320 337 320 337 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae tra-2</italic>
###xml 347 349 347 349 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b34">34</xref>
###xml 383 394 383 394 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 434 451 434 451 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae tra-2</italic>
###xml 511 513 511 513 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b21">21</xref>
###xml 531 542 531 542 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 0 11 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 69 80 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 189 199 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 221 231 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 305 315 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 320 331 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 383 394 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 434 445 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 531 542 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
C. briggsae GLD-1 may still function as a translational repressor of C. briggsae tra-2 mRNA even in the absence of a FOG-2 ortholog. This is a possibility because FOG-2 is not required for C. elegans GLD-1 binding to the C. elegans tra-2 mRNA in vitro [25], and some conservation is preserved between the C. elegans and C. briggsae tra-2 3' UTRs [34]. In this case, RNAi of GLD-1 in C. briggsae might feminize the germline given that C. briggsae tra-2 promotes female development in both the germline and soma [21]. Alternatively, C. briggsae GLD-1 might have no role in germline sex determination, in which case RNAi would not result in a sex determination phenotype.
###end p 41
###begin p 42
###xml 14 31 14 31 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae gld-1</italic>
###xml 74 82 74 82 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g005">Figure 5</xref>
###xml 93 100 93 100 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pbio-0030006-t002">Table 2</xref>
###xml 237 258 237 258 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 391 396 391 396 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 498 506 498 506 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g005">Figure 5</xref>
###xml 524 535 524 535 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 674 682 674 682 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g005">Figure 5</xref>
###xml 742 747 742 747 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 756 767 756 767 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 818 829 818 829 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 1011 1021 1011 1021 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 1114 1119 1114 1119 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">tra-2</italic>
###xml 14 25 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 524 535 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 756 767 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 818 829 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 1011 1021 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
Surprisingly, C. briggsae gld-1 RNAi resulted in a masculinized germline (Figure 5A, bottom; Table 2), with no effect on the soma. Staining with 4',6'-diamidino-2-phenylindole hydrochloride (DAPI) and anti-major sperm protein (MSP) (see Materials and Methods) revealed continuous spermatogenesis leading to a vast excess of sperm at the expense of oogenesis. Anti-GLD-1 antibody staining of gld-1 RNAi F1 gonad arms indicated that the level of GLD-1 protein was reduced to below detectable limits (Figure 5A, bottom right). C. briggsae control hermaphrodites injected with double-stranded RNA for green fluorescent protein (GFP) had gonad morphology identical to wild-type (Figure 5A, top left and middle left). The masculinized phenotype of gld-1 RNAi in C. briggsae indicates that the wild-type function of GLD-1 in C. briggsae is to promote the female germ cell fate, likely by the translational repression of an mRNA that encodes a masculinizing gene product. This function is in direct contrast to that of C. elegans GLD-1, which promotes the male germ cell fate by translational repression of the feminizing tra-2 mRNA.
###end p 42
###begin title 43
GLD-1 Function in Meiotic Prophase Progression during Oogenesis Is Conserved
###end title 43
###begin p 44
###xml 72 82 72 82 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 87 98 87 98 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 227 232 227 232 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 236 246 236 246 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 419 424 419 424 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rme-2</italic>
###xml 432 434 432 434 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b28">28</xref>
###xml 435 437 435 437 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b31">31</xref>
###xml 72 82 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 87 98 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 236 246 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
Given the difference in sex determination function, it is possible that C. elegans and C. briggsae GLD-1 have few conserved functions in germline development. To investigate this we took advantage of well-defined activities of gld-1 in C. elegans such as its essential function in female meiotic prophase progression and in the translational repression of the evolutionarily conserved yolk receptor mRNA encoded by the rme-2 locus [28,31].
###end p 44
###begin p 45
###xml 4 9 4 9 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 110 112 110 112 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b28">28</xref>
###xml 113 115 113 115 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b29">29</xref>
###xml 228 230 228 230 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b28">28</xref>
###xml 231 233 231 233 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b29">29</xref>
###xml 273 278 273 278 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 287 298 287 298 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 359 375 359 375 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans gld-1</italic>
###xml 471 473 471 473 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b29">29</xref>
###xml 520 525 520 525 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-3</italic>
###xml 536 541 536 541 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 550 561 550 561 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 569 585 569 585 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans fog-3</italic>
###xml 649 666 649 666 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae fog-3</italic>
###xml 713 715 713 715 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b42">42</xref>
###xml 736 753 736 753 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae fog-3</italic>
###xml 820 837 820 837 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae gld-1</italic>
###xml 287 298 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 359 369 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 550 561 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 569 579 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 649 660 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 736 747 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 820 831 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
The gld-1-null tumorous phenotype results from aberrant oogenic prophase progression and a return to mitosis [28,29]. This phenotype is dependent on germline sex because a tumor only occurs when germ cell fate is set to female [28,29]. The masculinized phenotype caused by gld-1 RNAi in C. briggsae is likely to preclude the detection of this function as the C. elegans gld-1-null tumorous phenotype is suppressed by mutations that cause masculinization of the germline [29]. To overcome the masculinization we combined fog-3 RNAi with gld-1 RNAi in C. briggsae. Since C. elegans fog-3 functions near the end of the sex determination pathway and in C. briggsae fog-3 RNAi results in feminization of the germline [42], we predicted that C. briggsae fog-3 RNAi would be epistatic to the masculinization of the germline of C. briggsae gld-1 RNAi.
###end p 45
###begin p 46
###xml 15 31 15 31 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans gld-1</italic>
###xml 46 51 46 51 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 55 60 55 60 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 65 70 65 70 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-3</italic>
###xml 74 84 74 84 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 104 109 104 109 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 114 119 114 119 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-3</italic>
###xml 123 134 123 134 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 181 189 181 189 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g005">Figure 5</xref>
###xml 192 199 192 199 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pbio-0030006-t002">Table 2</xref>
###xml 220 225 220 225 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-3</italic>
###xml 281 283 281 283 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b42">42</xref>
###xml 442 450 442 450 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g005">Figure 5</xref>
###xml 695 697 695 697 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b56">56</xref>
###xml 744 755 744 755 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 814 819 814 819 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 858 863 858 863 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 868 873 868 873 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-3</italic>
###xml 938 943 938 943 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 15 25 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 74 84 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 123 134 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 744 755 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
Similar to the C. elegans gld-1-null, RNAi of gld-1 or gld-1 and fog-3 in C. elegans and double RNAi of gld-1 and fog-3 in C. briggsae resulted in a robust proximal germline tumor (Figure 5B; Table 2). Control RNAi with fog-3 alone resulted in feminized germlines in both species [42]. Both the mitotic zone and transition zone appear to have roughly normal nuclear morphology, with more proximal nuclei having abnormal pachytene morphology (Figure 5B), suggesting that germ cells are entering meiosis but progressing aberrantly before returning to mitosis. The return-to-mitosis tumorous phenotype in each species was confirmed using phosphohistone H3 staining, a mitotic proliferation marker [56]. We cannot rule out the possibility that the C. briggsae phenotypes observed, masculinization of the germline with gld-1 RNAi alone and tumorous germline with gld-1 and fog-3 RNAi, are the result of incomplete knockdown leading to partial gld-1 loss of function.
###end p 46
###begin p 47
###xml 4 9 4 9 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rme-2</italic>
###xml 93 103 93 103 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 105 107 105 107 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b31">31</xref>
###xml 113 124 113 124 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans,</italic>
###xml 193 198 193 198 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rme-2</italic>
###xml 362 364 362 364 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b31">31</xref>
###xml 370 386 370 386 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans gld-1</italic>
###xml 541 546 541 546 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rme-2</italic>
###xml 553 555 553 555 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b31">31</xref>
###xml 93 103 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 113 123 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 370 380 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
The rme-2 yolk receptor mRNA is a known target of GLD-1-mediated translational repression in C. elegans [31]. In C. elegans, GLD-1 and RME-2 have mutually exclusive expression patterns because rme-2 mRNA is translationally repressed in the transition zone and pachytene region, where GLD-1 levels are high, and translated in oocytes, where GLD-1 levels are low [31]. In C. elegans gld-1-null germlines RME-2 is ectopically expressed in the transition zone and pachytene region owing to loss of GLD-1-mediated translational repression of the rme-2 mRNA [31].
###end p 47
###begin p 48
###xml 54 65 54 65 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 80 91 80 91 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 130 147 130 147 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae rme-2</italic>
###xml 154 162 154 162 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g006">Figure 6</xref>
###xml 186 197 186 197 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 218 223 218 223 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rme-2</italic>
###xml 245 250 245 250 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 255 260 255 260 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-3</italic>
###xml 339 341 339 341 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b57">57</xref>
###xml 442 452 442 452 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 457 468 457 468 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 470 478 470 478 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g006">Figure 6</xref>
###xml 554 559 554 559 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rme-2</italic>
###xml 54 65 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 80 91 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 130 141 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 186 197 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 442 452 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 457 468 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
A similar, mutually exclusive accumulation pattern in C. briggsae suggests that C. briggsae GLD-1 is a translational repressor of C. briggsae rme-2 mRNA (Figure 6). To determine whether C. briggsae GLD-1 represses the rme-2 mRNA, double RNAi of gld-1 and fog-3 was performed in both species, and gonad arms were stained for RME-2 protein [57]. Reduction of GLD-1 and FOG-3 by RNAi results in the ectopic accumulation of RME-2 protein in both C. elegans and C. briggsae (Figure 6), indicating that the role of GLD-1 in the translational repression of the rme-2 mRNA is conserved. Thus, despite the opposite roles of GLD-1 in sex determination, essential functions of GLD-1 in oogenesis are conserved between the species.
###end p 48
###begin title 49
Discussion
###end title 49
###begin p 50
###xml 125 135 125 135 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 140 151 140 151 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 180 185 180 185 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">tra-2</italic>
###xml 264 275 264 275 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans,</italic>
###xml 337 348 337 348 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 461 462 461 462 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">.</italic>
###xml 504 509 504 509 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 536 542 536 542 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">ftr-1,</italic>
###xml 558 563 558 563 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 615 625 615 625 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 912 922 912 922 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 995 1006 995 1006 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 1024 1034 1024 1034 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 1269 1279 1269 1279 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 1284 1295 1284 1295 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 125 135 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 140 151 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 264 274 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 337 348 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 615 625 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 912 922 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 995 1006 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 1024 1034 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 1269 1279 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 1284 1295 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
Our results indicate that the control of hermaphrodite spermatogenesis is fundamentally different between the sister species C. elegans and C. briggsae at the level of FOG-2/GLD-1/tra-2 mRNA regulation. While FOG-2 is essential for self-fertile hermaphroditism in C. elegans, a closely related homolog of FOG-2 could not be recovered in C. briggsae by reciprocal best BLAST, phylogenetic inference, low-stringency hybridization, or analysis of conserved synteny. Comparison of synonymous changes between fog-2 and its closest relative, ftr-1, indicates that fog-2 is the product of a recent expansion "specific" to C. elegans in the FTR gene family and implies that the evolution of FOG-2 and its incorporation into the sex determination pathway occurred post-speciation. Consistent with this, the C-terminal region of FOG-2 required for binding to GLD-1 was found to be highly diverged and "unique" to FOG-2 in C. elegans. Interestingly, GLD-1 was found to have a sex determination function in C. briggsae opposite that in C. elegans while retaining similar functions in female meiotic prophase progression and oogenesis. The absence of FOG-2, and the opposite sex determination function of GLD-1, provides evidence for the independent evolution of hermaphroditism in C. elegans and C. briggsae.
###end p 50
###begin title 51
General Conservation of the Sex Determination Pathway
###end title 51
###begin p 52
###xml 37 47 37 47 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 52 63 52 63 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 154 207 154 207 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae her-1, tra-2, fem-1, fem-2, fem-3, fog-3,</italic>
###xml 212 217 212 217 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">tra-1</italic>
###xml 264 274 264 274 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 335 337 335 337 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b17">17</xref>
###xml 338 340 338 340 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b21">21</xref>
###xml 341 343 341 343 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b26">26</xref>
###xml 344 346 344 346 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b41">41</xref>
###xml 347 349 347 349 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b42">42</xref>
###xml 350 352 350 352 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b43">43</xref>
###xml 353 355 353 355 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b45">45</xref>
###xml 37 47 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 52 63 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 154 165 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 264 274 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
Reciprocal best BLAST indicates that C. elegans and C. briggsae have orthologs of 30 of 31 known sex determination pathway genes. Conserved functions for C. briggsae her-1, tra-2, fem-1, fem-2, fem-3, fog-3, and tra-1 have been demonstrated by transgene rescue of C. elegans mutations or similarity of RNAi loss-of-function phenotype [17,21,26,41,42,43,45]. The general conservation of genes that govern sex determination suggests that the underlying pathway remains largely intact between the species.
###end p 52
###begin p 53
###xml 58 63 58 63 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fem-2</italic>
###xml 68 73 68 73 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fem-3</italic>
###xml 179 190 179 190 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 219 221 219 221 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b41">41</xref>
###xml 222 224 222 224 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b45">45</xref>
###xml 486 496 486 496 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 501 512 501 512 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 624 635 624 635 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 649 659 649 659 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 798 803 798 803 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">tra-2</italic>
###xml 821 826 821 826 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fem-3</italic>
###xml 957 959 957 959 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b41">41</xref>
###xml 179 190 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 486 496 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 501 512 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 624 635 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 649 659 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
RNAi and transgenic experiments have suggested that while fem-2 and fem-3 have conserved roles in the somatic sex determination of both species, they may play diminished roles in C. briggsae germline sex determination [41,45]. There are two possibilities that could explain these results. One is that there are inherent species-specific differences in susceptibility to RNAi or in the ability to reconstitute complete gene function by transgene rescue. The other is that differences in C. elegans and C. briggsae phenotypes reveal functional divergence in sex determination pathway components. Analysis of null mutations in C. briggsae orthologs of C. elegans sex determination genes will help to distinguish between these possibilities. While some functional differences may turn out to be valid, tra-2 (feminizing) and fem-3 (masculinizing) apparently play the same somatic roles in both species, and their epistatic relationship appears to be conserved [41].
###end p 53
###begin title 54
###xml 0 5 0 5 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 19 29 19 29 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 19 29 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
fog-2 Is Unique to C. elegans
###end title 54
###begin p 55
###xml 141 146 141 146 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 150 161 150 161 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 177 182 177 182 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 216 226 216 226 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 293 309 293 309 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans fog-2</italic>
###xml 346 351 346 351 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 374 376 374 376 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b25">25</xref>
###xml 428 439 428 439 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 467 472 467 472 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">tra-2</italic>
###xml 537 542 537 542 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 596 606 596 606 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 644 656 644 656 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae,</italic>
###xml 732 743 732 743 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 799 809 799 809 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 150 161 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 216 226 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 293 303 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 428 439 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 596 606 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 644 655 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 732 743 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 799 809 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
Within the context of general conservation of sex determination pathway components and conserved key epistatic relationships, the absence of fog-2 in C. briggsae is intriguing. fog-2 arose as a consequence of recent C. elegans-specific gene duplication events, and none of the closely related C. elegans fog-2 paralogs can compensate for loss of fog-2 in sex determination [25]. Thus, it is unlikely that more distantly related C. briggsae FTRs are involved in GLD-1/tra-2-mRNA-mediated promotion of hermaphrodite spermatogenesis. Since fog-2 is essential for the promotion of spermatogenesis in C. elegans hermaphrodites and is not present in C. briggsae, the direct implication is that specification of the male germ cell fate in C. briggsae hermaphrodites is fundamentally different from that in C. elegans and that it evolved independently.
###end p 55
###begin p 56
###xml 169 177 169 177 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g004">Figure 4</xref>
###xml 313 323 313 323 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 355 360 355 360 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 416 421 416 421 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">ftr-1</italic>
###xml 474 479 474 479 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">ftr-1</italic>
###xml 518 523 518 523 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 583 592 583 592 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="sg002">Figure S2</xref>
###xml 599 604 599 604 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">ftr-1</italic>
###xml 674 679 674 679 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">ftr-1</italic>
###xml 689 694 689 694 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 775 777 775 777 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b25">25</xref>
###xml 313 323 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
The highly diverged C-terminus of FOG-2 is under positive selection and is necessary and sufficient for GLD-1 binding within the context of an F-box and FTH domain (see Figure 4). Acquiring the diverged C-terminus was crucial in FOG-2 becoming incorporated into the sex determination pathway. With respect to the C. elegans lineage, it is unclear whether fog-2 retains an ancestral function in sex determination and ftr-1 has changed/drifted away or, alternatively, whether ftr-1 represents the ancestral function and fog-2 has recently evolved a role in sex determination (also see Figure S2). The ftr-1 gene is expressed, though its function is currently unknown. RNAi of ftr-1 into the fog-2 null did not reveal any obvious phenotypes beyond feminization of the germline [25].
###end p 56
###begin title 57
###xml 29 39 29 39 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 44 55 44 55 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 29 39 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 44 55 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
Conserved GLD-1 Functions in C. elegans and C. briggsae Meiotic Prophase during Oogenesis
###end title 57
###begin p 58
###xml 117 126 117 126 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g005">Figures 5</xref>
###xml 131 132 131 132 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g006">6</xref>
###xml 213 223 213 223 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 228 239 228 239 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 274 279 274 279 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rme-2</italic>
###xml 346 354 346 354 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pbio-0030006-g006">Figure 6</xref>
###xml 384 394 384 394 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 476 478 476 478 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b31">31</xref>
###xml 479 481 479 481 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b55">55</xref>
###xml 544 560 544 560 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans gld-1</italic>
###xml 645 647 645 647 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b31">31</xref>
###xml 714 719 714 719 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gld-1</italic>
###xml 781 798 781 798 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae gld-1</italic>
###xml 803 808 803 808 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-3</italic>
###xml 904 915 904 915 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 988 999 988 999 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 1133 1138 1133 1138 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">tra-2</italic>
###xml 1151 1153 1151 1153 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b25">25</xref>
###xml 1154 1156 1154 1156 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b27">27</xref>
###xml 1157 1159 1157 1159 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b31">31</xref>
###xml 1160 1162 1160 1162 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b55">55</xref>
###xml 1163 1165 1163 1165 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b58">58</xref>
###xml 213 223 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 228 239 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 384 394 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 544 554 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 781 792 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 904 915 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 988 999 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
GLD-1 function in meiotic prophase progression and oogenesis shows substantial conservation between the species (see Figures 5 and 6), which is not surprising given the high level of sequence conservation between C. elegans and C. briggsae GLD-1. This is illustrated by the rme-2 yolk receptor mRNA being regulated similarly between the species (Figure 6). Current data indicate that C. elegans GLD-1 binds to, and likely represses translation of, more than 100 mRNA targets [31,55] (M.-H. Lee, V. Reinke, and T. Schedl, unpublished data). The C. elegans gld-1-null tumorous phenotype likely results from misregulation of multiple mRNA targets [31]. While the identity of the misregulated mRNA targets causing the gld-1-null tumorous phenotype are currently unknown, the fact that C. briggsae gld-1 and fog-3 RNAi results in a similar tumorous phenotype suggests that a similar, if not identical, set of C. briggsae GLD-1 mRNA targets are misregulated. The absence of a FOG-2 ortholog in C. briggsae is unlikely to have a major effect on GLD-1-mediated translational control since FOG-2 appears to be required only as a cofactor for tra-2 repression [25,27,31,55,58]. Thus, it is possible that the majority of GLD-1 mRNA targets involved in prophase progression and oogenesis are regulated similarly between species.
###end p 58
###begin title 59
###xml 28 38 28 38 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 43 54 43 54 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 28 38 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 43 54 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
Divergent GLD-1 Function in C. elegans and C. briggsae Sex Determination
###end title 59
###begin p 60
###xml 30 40 30 40 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 45 56 45 56 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 118 128 118 128 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 166 177 166 177 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 264 275 264 275 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 317 322 317 322 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">tra-2</italic>
###xml 344 354 344 354 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 415 431 415 431 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans tra-2</italic>
###xml 481 483 481 483 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b24">24</xref>
###xml 518 528 518 528 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 533 544 533 544 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 569 574 569 574 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">tra-2</italic>
###xml 649 651 649 651 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b34">34</xref>
###xml 690 700 690 700 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 705 716 705 716 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 984 986 984 986 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b25">25</xref>
###xml 987 989 987 989 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b27">27</xref>
###xml 990 992 990 992 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b28">28</xref>
###xml 993 995 993 995 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b29">29</xref>
###xml 996 998 996 998 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b30">30</xref>
###xml 30 40 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 45 56 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 118 128 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 166 177 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 264 275 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 344 354 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 415 425 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 518 528 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 533 544 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 690 700 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 705 716 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
Genetic analysis reveals that C. elegans and C. briggsae GLD-1 have opposite functions in germline sex determination; C. elegans GLD-1 promotes spermatogenesis while C. briggsae GLD-1 promotes oogenesis. This indicates that the major sex determination function of C. briggsae GLD-1 is not translational repression of tra-2 feminizing activity. C. elegans GLD-1 binds two 28 nucleotide direct repeat elements on the C. elegans tra-2 mRNA 3' UTR to mediate translational repression [24]. Somatic reporter gene assays in C. elegans and C. briggsae have suggested that the tra-2 3' UTRs of both species are able to function in translational repression [34], with the implication being that the C. elegans and C. briggsae 3' UTRs are regulated similarly. However, these data are difficult to interpret in the context of germline sex determination, as GLD-1 and FOG-2 are not natively expressed in the soma and neither GLD-1 nor FOG-2 have essential functions in somatic sex determination [25,27,28,29,30].
###end p 60
###begin p 61
###xml 46 57 46 57 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 77 94 77 94 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae tra-2</italic>
###xml 188 198 188 198 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 231 241 231 241 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. elegans</named-content>
###xml 261 278 261 278 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae rme-2</italic>
###xml 326 327 326 327 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b02">2</xref>
###xml 328 330 328 330 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b31">31</xref>
###xml 331 333 331 333 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b55">55</xref>
###xml 334 336 334 336 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b58">58</xref>
###xml 337 339 337 339 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b59">59</xref>
###xml 430 446 430 446 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans tra-2</italic>
###xml 456 467 456 467 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans,</italic>
###xml 487 492 487 492 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">tra-2</italic>
###xml 516 521 516 521 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fog-2</italic>
###xml 592 594 592 594 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pbio-0030006-b25">25</xref>
###xml 687 703 687 703 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans tra-2</italic>
###xml 782 793 782 793 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 806 823 806 823 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae tra-2</italic>
###xml 46 57 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 77 88 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 188 198 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 231 241 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 261 272 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 430 440 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 456 466 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 687 697 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 782 793 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
###xml 806 817 <span type="species:ncbi:6238">C. briggsae</span>
One hypothesis to explain our results is that C. briggsae GLD-1 binds to the C. briggsae tra-2 mRNA but is necessary for translational activation instead of translational repression as in C. elegans. However, for all characterized C. elegans GLD-1 targets, and C. briggsae rme-2 mRNA, GLD-1 acts as a translational repressor [2,31,55,58,59]. We currently do not understand how FOG-2 acts with GLD-1 in translational repression of C. elegans tra-2 mRNA. In C. elegans, GLD-1 can bind the tra-2 mRNA in the absence of fog-2 in worm extracts but cannot properly repress its translation in vivo [25]. This suggests that the role of FOG-2 may be to recruit additional factors specific to the C. elegans tra-2 mRNA 3' UTR that allow for efficient GLD-1 translational repression. Assuming C. briggsae GLD-1 binds C. briggsae tra-2 mRNA in vivo, given the absence of a FOG-2 ortholog, there may be no regulatory consequence of this binding.
###end p 61
###begin p 62
###xml 28 39 28 39 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 225 237 225 237 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. briggsae,</italic>
###xml 270 281 270 281 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
###xml 373 378 373 378 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rme-2</italic>
###xml 458 469 458 469 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="genus-species">C. briggsae</named-content>
